0000000000000000	BHFPPA01	Prospecting Plan	a	the				Default prospecting stanza. Use it preferably in combination with other stanzas to make raw material sources appear around. For instance, without a 'Find Better Materials' stanza, you will only find Basic raw materials. The sources you find have a 2.5 s extraction time bonus, compared to natural raw material sources.	
0000000000000000	BHFSPA01	Spying Plan	a	the				Spying base plan stanza for foraging	
0000000000000000	BHFPPOA01	Terrain Specializing	a	the				Finds sources with higher amount of material; uses less focus to track deposits.	 
0000000000000000	BHFPPOB01	Material Specializing	a	the				Chooses the raw material you want to find.	 
0000000000000000	BHFPPOC01	Range +	a	the				Extends the range of source prospection.	 
0000000000000000	BHFPPOD01	Cone Angle +	a	the				Extends the cone of source prospection.	 
0000000000000000	BHFPPOE01	Multiple Spot +	a	the				Finds more than one forage source.	 
0000000000000000	BHFPPOF01	Knowledge +	a	the				Gets more information about forage sources.	 
0000000000000000	BHFPPOG01	Speed +	a	the				Prospects faster.	 
0000000000000000	BHFPPOH01	Source Time +	a	the				Extends the extraction time of the sources.	 
0000000000000000	BHFPPOI01	Find Better Materials	a	the				Finds better raw materials (without this stanza you will find only basic raw material).	 
0000000000000000	BHFPPOK01	Deposit tracking	a	the				Tracks the nearest raw material deposit in the region, matching the properties set in your action. Use this stanza preferably in combination with other stanzas, to locate deposits containing specific raw materials. For instance, without a 'Find Better Materials' stanza, you will only find Basic raw materials. Please note that a deposit may contain several raw materials, therefore once you have found the deposit, you still need to prospect to find the particular place(s) corresponding to the raw material you are searching for.	Track raw material deposits.
